 chapter one charlotte we were flying over canada when the panic set in . 
 i felt a mild tightening in my chest as i thought about the plane that was taking me closer to the place so unimaginably full of memories that i could n't quite process it .

 kevin moved through life with an almost effortless ease , usually getting exactly what he wanted without even contemplating another outcome .

 i had been wide-awake for the entire flight .

 liam .
